padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2321990" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Mandie731"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2128810"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2128810.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Mandie731" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chloe/Nomade-Eau-de-Toilette-53224.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.53224.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Nomade Eau de Toilette"title="Nomade Eau de Toilette"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2321990ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2321990" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2128810">Mandie731</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-20"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729451923" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If Delina was a person she would have been the popular girl at school.  The one that everyone secretly envied because not only was she beautiful but she was also a really lovely person who was kind to other people.  She formed positive, healthy relationships with others because her parents were great role models and loved and respected each other.  Now, as an adult, she lives a fulfilling life in a career that she has flourished in.  She is happily married and wakes up each morning with a smile on her face, bathed in sunshine and ready to continue her perfect life.  And herein lies the problem and the reason I can't love Delina; she is just too perfect.  She is someone I could never be, and to even try would be exhausting.  <br />
<br />
Having said that, when I am in the right frame of mind, I like to think that I can rock this fragrance.  She is a special occasion type of scent for sure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2321990"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2321990#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1398132">marshmallowbunny</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-19">10/19/24 10:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Another incredibly overhyped fragrance. This is just a strong, bitter rhubarb and a very synthetic rose. I have finally decided that if a fragrance has rhubarb in the notes, chances are I’m not going to enjoy it. Rhubarb gives perfumes  a masculine edge that I’m not really into, especially when it’s mixed with fruity/gourmand notes that are stereotypically very sweet and feminine leaning. The contrast between two strong top notes on different ends of the perfume spectrum is overwhelming. Due to its sharp and sour qualities, rhubarb can very easily dominate a perfume and that’s exactly what’s happened with Delina. Also, the price tag on this is absolutely insane. They took the scent DNA of Chloé Roses, threw in some random notes and then said “Ah, yes! this is is $400!” Lol no… Chloé Roses is better and far more affordable. Sometimes less is more. Love the bottle on this one though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2320829"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2320829#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2320345" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s beautiful, well blended, very crowd pleasing fruity rose but it’s boring. There’s something a little stale about the rose note that makes it feel a little dated as well. I understand why so many people like it - it’s not offensive and the olfactory embodiment of “pretty”. It’s also versatile, I wore it regularly when I had the sample simply because the people around me loved it and it’s easy to wear for almost any occasion. I understand cementing it as a classic, everyone likes it but it’s honestly nothing revolutionary - it’s just a blend of notes most people like, pleasant but boring.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I much prefer creamy woodsy unisex scents that lean into green and smokey notes, so this sharp sweet fruity explosion is FAR out of my comfort zone, but I wanted to test it for my sister so here we are. <br />
<br />
Objectively this is a gorgeous scent. The predominant smell to me is a pleasantly acidic zingy rhubarb that really cuts through your senses, with a comforting rose cushion in the background. What is most impressive though is the silage. I gave myself a single spray on my wrist and the smell is filling the whole room. I can't even smell the other scent I spritzed on my other wrist without getting hit with waves of tart rhubarb. It's so not me (my current go-to has been Naked Dance by Oddity for frame of reference), so I would never purchase a full size, but for someone who wants a big bright feminine scent that will leave an impact, I imagine this is perfect.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2300046" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ville I"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2235353"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2235353.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ville I" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2300046ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2300046" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2235353">Ville I</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-30">09/30/24 08:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I personally love this scent. It is so beautiful I get emotional every time I smell it. However, there are some things to consider before buying.<br />
<br />
I got this for my wife (ok, that is a lie, I wanted it for my collection) but she doesn´t really wear it all that much and I can understand why. It is not one bit sexy or seductive. When a woman wears a scent, that scent is supposed to express her femininity, womanhood or whatever you want to call it. At least where I live, very few women would feel that a bunch of pretty pretty flowers are a true expression of what their femininity is, and they don´t wear perfumes to appreciate the level of perfumery that has gone into Delina, they do it to feel desired. Delina is the ultimate good and clean girl that could never do anything wrong, and the women I know who have smelled this all say the same thing: this is not me.<br />
<br />
Take something like Atomic Rose by Initio. It is 75-80% Delina, but they have turned it darker, dirtier, more masculine and way more sexier. Delina is the more beautiful scent and objectively Delina is better perfumery: the notes open up better and sound brighter, but I bet most women would prefer to smell like Atomic Rose regardless.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2277171" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="candi_n_spice"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1491103"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1491103.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="candi_n_spice" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Estee-Lauder/Modern-Muse-Le-Rouge-Gloss-38990.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.38990.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Modern Muse Le Rouge Gloss"title="Modern Muse Le Rouge Gloss"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2277171ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2277171" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1491103">candi_n_spice</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-09">09/09/24 13:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Okay, I get it, lol. Been waiting to get my nose on this for awhile, but hesitated due to the price, and the reviews that say it's not special. It might not reinvent the wheel, but it sure does smell fantastic! I just received a large decant order, and was forced to try it first, as half of it had leaked out. Of course, since it was the most expensive one I ordered and I'd planned to savor each drop. 😭 Anyway, the little baggie it was in was wet with it, so I cut it open and smeared it on. <br />
<br />
Even before identifying the source of the leak, it was clear that it had been something with roses. The rose note is very prominent, especially on the opening, rosy and fruity. That alone, while obviously done well here, isn't very exciting. But Delina does what pretty much all of my favorite frags do, it balances that sweet fruity floral opening with spice, vanilla, wood, and incense as it develops on the skin. She might be the pretty popular girl, but she has depth. I can't stop smelling my arm. I honestly hate it when I love something expensive enough to actually want more after the sample, this happened with Lira, lol. I'll probably look for a deal on a bigger decant, and/or try the Andromeda's Moon version, at least until I'm a bit richer. 🤭 <br />
<br />
I am more tempted to stick with the real thing with this one, just bc the potency and longevity are definitely there. Be careful with overspraying, it's the type that can become unpleasant when overdone. To me that translates to good value, just use less. <br />
<br />
It should go without saying to not try this if you don't like the smell of roses! Otherwise, I absolutely see why it's so popular. I have seen some say it's sharp, but it's not sharp to me in an unpleasant way like certain notes can be. Especially ambroxan. I'd say it's more of a tartness, largely from the rhubarb. Which keeps it from being overly heavy with rose and sweetness, imo. I think most people would find this pleasant, and any age can wear it. Lovely. 🌹</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2277171"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2277171#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276740" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
At first, when I got a tester for Delina, I was on the fence. It hit me with an explosion of roses and litchi. Thirty minutes in, it settles into this rose cloud, with softer litchi note and a hint of peony. Delina does not develop too much on my skin, it stays as that rosy powdery cloud throughout the day and even through the evening, if I am going out. It smells great on warm and sunny days, however on hot days it can get a bit overpowering. <br />
<br />
From the downside, I will mention the price and, if you are not a fan of roses, you should skip it. In my opinion, it should not be a blind buy either.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2276740"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2276740#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276103" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2161286">makinmagic1</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-03">09/03/24 17:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I wanted to not like it. It is arguably the most popular perfume in the world right now, so many people are obsessed with it. I wanted to believe that I am more sophisticated than this, that I will not go with the crowd. Well... I now completely get the fascination with this scent. It's splendid. It's quite simple, and from the first sniff you know that it is indeed amazing. It doesn't need time to "mature" or "develop" or to be worn in the right weather and season, it's straight out gorgeous from the first second. <br />
The rose is very prominent, and to me it's very fresh and slightly sugary, sort of similar to La Fille de Berlin's rose. This baby rose is very pretty, but I think it's ever so slightly tart and sour litchee that truly makes it stand out. It sort of gives it smooth watery (but not watered down) vibe? I kind of get "gelatinous" rose effect because of it. Nutmeg is also quite noticeable and gives it a slight sharp edge. <br />
When I spray it, I definitely get projection. I just used 10 sprays while being at home and have been sitting is this glorious rosey cloud for 2 hours. I absolutely adore this! Yes, this one is popular for a reason.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2270599"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2270599#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2270098" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2055934">Lbustos2</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 16:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Personally, this smells like Lush’s Rose Jam perfume. Take this review with a grain of salt, but both seem quite similar to me. <br />
<br />
Delina is a sugary, floral, syrupy rose with some powder dusted on top. I will say this perfume is unforgettable and once you’ve smelled it once, you’ll be able to pick it out of room or detect it while walking through the grocery aisles at Trader Joe’s. At least, that’s what happened to me. <br />
<br />
This perfume is so darling and I can see why it’s so dang expensive. I 100% recommend if you like to smell like, sweet, jammy roses… purchase her! I will say, one of my colleagues purchased the Rich Auntie body oil from Brown Sugar Babe and I totally think they smell identical. I will say the body oil projects like crazy. Whewwwwww you’ll be a walking cloud of Delina if you use the body oil. <br />
<br />
Not trying to push the product, but I was sold and ended up purchasing the oil. I’m glad I did. Delina is a beautiful scent that makes me feel like I’m a princess in Bridgerton. It makes me feel like I’m going to high tea with my friends while wearing a poofy dress and a tiara. This perfume quite literally makes me feel like Princess Peach.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2259879"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2259879#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2259850" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; ✔️❌ Mugler Angel Nova: the sillage isn’t as sweet, otherwise they’re quite similar<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1781065">monipod</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-07">08/07/24 05:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I let Delina go under the radar for a long time as I'm not a huge floral/fruit fan, though whenever I tried it on paper, it smelt lovely. I finally decided to get a travel sized spray and wow... It's just beautiful on skin. I fell in love immediately. The Turkish Rose reminds me of Annick Goutal's Ce Soir Ou Jamais but the fruit burst is a nice point of difference in the beginning. The other middle notes aren't obvious to me but I think it's the overall combination that is giving me a certain something that I'm liking. I don't feel like it's dried down properly yet (after 6+ hours) but I'm vaguely picking up some cedar now. It's a powerhouse of a frag as well. I can still smell it as though I just sprayed it moments ago. Fortunately it just continues to be a pleasing scent. <br />
<br />
Sometimes the hype about a fragrance is due to it being universally enjoyable: it's not that there's something super amazing or unique about it necessarily. Delina is (in the best possible way) inoffensive and safe. You could blind buy this and even if you somehow hate it, you'll easily find someone who will happily take it off you. Granted, if you're not a fan of rose at all, Delina may not be for you, but I think it's worth a try.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2241541"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2241541#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2240470" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; For a rose lover like myself, this is the most perfect rose garden concentrated in a bottle. Imagine sticking your nose is a perfectly scented pink rose, and you got Delina. A bit wet, humid, green, with some juiciness of the lychees and a tough of vanilla. That's it. Simple and perfect, feminine, delicate but not weak, in an adorable pink bottle. Sadly, very expensive. It feels so "me" . I adore it. I would like a bathtub full of it. On a different note, it smells quite similar to Chloe edt version, the original one, except this has some vanilla in the mix, and it is stronger. Highly recommended to any rose lover. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/878296">lauren.ingham</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-14">07/14/24 23:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I love Delina, but it does not love me... If you are sensitive to certain fragrances, leave this one alone. Gives me a headache and makes me feel a little nauseous :(</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2218884"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2218884#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2213286" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2213286" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Bronstet"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1698991"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Bronstet" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2213286ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2213286" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1698991">Bronstet</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-09">07/09/24 14:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>* Beautiful and unique combination of sweet, rose, tropical fruit, musk and spice aromas<br />
* Very good performer<br />
* Pleasant and fragrant<br />
* Very smooth to the nose<br />
* Versatile; great for all ages and occasions <br />
<br />
* Too feminine for a man to wear even if one uses unisex fragrances<br />
* May come off smelling too much like candy to some users<br />
* Not good for those who dislike sweet fragrances<br />
* Could have used a fresher and/or darker note (which is in fact what Delina Exclusif does) to be either more uplifting or more mysterious <br />
* Expensive<br />
<br />
I received a sample of Parfum de Marley's runaway hit Delina as a bonus from an online discounter after placing a large order with them. I thought it was an odd thing to include for a straight male but was happy to give it a try. I'm glad I did. This is an absolutely beautiful and unique fragrance. It combines the tropical fruit of an Aventus or Bade'e al Oud Sublime and blends it with the rose of a Tom Ford Rose Prick and holds it all together with floral musk and light spice aromas. This is extremely pleasant and fragrant to the nose, and has quite a noticeably smooth texture on the nostrils. It's versatile and good for all occasions and ages, I'd be just as happy smelling if off of my young nieces, my sisters, my friends and even my grandmothers. Performance is strong, too. <br />
<br />
The catch here of course is that as a straight male I absolutely cannot see myself wearing this and was genuinely puzzled as to why I received this sample. Look, I have no problem using not just unisex fragrances of all kinds (fruit, gourmand, rose), and I even rock a couple that are blatantly marketed strictly to women -- Dior Hypnotic Poison and Givenchy L'Interdit Rouge -- and have actually been told I smell nice by other straight male friends when using them! :D But I do actually have to draw the line with Delina. I love the idea of smelling this fragrance off of a woman but not the idea of using it myself. It just leans far too feminine, which is actually what it was clearly intended to do. So no issue there. I think it's a really good perfume and, again, I would love to smell this off of a woman. <br />
<br />
This is quite sweet and is not good for you if you dislike sweet fragrances. It may come off as smelling like candy to you. It could've have used either an uplifting fresh note or a more mysterious darker note. I understand that Delina Exclusif in fact did just that by adding a  touch of incense and oud so obviously someone else thinks the same. <br />
<br />
More concerning than that for women, if we're being totally honest, is that it is rather expensive as are all Parfum de Marley creations. You are looking at approximately $US 200/$CAD 270 at online discounters and  $US 375/$500 CAD at retail which IMHO is quite a lot for a single bottle of perfume or cologne. It is a niche fragrance from a niche house so do expect to pay niche prices wherever you get it from. <br />
<br />
With that said, if you can afford it, it is a beautiful fragrance so feel free to rock it. When I was young, our garden had lot of rhubarbs, so for my nose this is rhubarb bomb. Rhubarb tartness is obvious which I love. After that comes aquatic and fruity. I'm rose lover, but it's very soft and not in the mane role. So I think if you don't like rose note, you still can enjoy Delina. After few ours on my skin it comes more sweet and I can smell vanilla and cashmeran. Luckily I do not smell incense which is not my cup of tea. It's not skin scent and you have to be careful, you can put too much and it can come overwhelming. Clothes it last eternal and my skin I can smell it even after 12 hours. I think if you live warm climate, it's softer but in the North it can be too much in winter time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2192070"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2192070#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2191336" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The original Delina is by far my favorite of the three. It starts out somewhat Juicy and Tart, but ultimately it has the most beautiful Rose scent that stands out above all else. It has a sweetness; a fruity sweetness, not a sugary sweetness. It's so lovely that I would wear this year round as a day scent. Although most people would categorize it as a spring and summer scent. A very similar, but more affordable perfume is Viva la Rose by Juicy Couture. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2177549" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="CarmenNola23"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1653181"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1653181.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="CarmenNola23" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Gucci/Gucci-Bloom-44894.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.44894.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gucci Bloom"title="Gucci Bloom"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2177549ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2177549" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1653181">CarmenNola23</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-04">06/04/24 06:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have worn Delina for a few months now as I wanted to wait and really experience it before giving a detailed review. When I first sampled it, I couldn’t help but think of Chloe. I am shocked it’s not listed in the fragrances of similarity. If Chloe is a young, syrupy rose-Delina is her older, spicier sister.  A litchi/ rose/ woody mix is hardly a breakthrough in modern perfumes, but there’s something special about Delina. The sweet rose and incense hit hard in the opening, but almost immediately the creamy cashmere mellows the spiciness- softening its rough edges. The peony and citrus make a lasting bouquet that lingers and projects for hours. The finish is a strawberry jam rose elevated by woody vetiver and rounded out by powdery clean musk. In the seemingly unending trend of vanilla gourmand lately (if that’s your thing, go for the Exclusif) Delina both takes me back to beautiful, floral femininity in fragrance but is also unique and worthy of a place in any collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It is very girly and sweet. It is a safe blind buy if you like rose scents. For me is the better than Delina Exclusive as it is has a more mature profile. The longevity on my skin is not great and I can barely smell it after the first hour. The most prominent note for me is the rose. I do think it is a bit overpriced but if you are into your floral scents is worth having it in your collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2170172"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2170172#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2167625" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; At this point, I don’t know how I can live without this perfume. I’m savouring the last bits I have because I know I will buy another bottle, but the price tag is heavy. There’s a good reason it is so popular and I believe that even though it is, it is insanely unique. You cannot compare to the DNA of BR540, where you smell it everywhere. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2141473" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jow012"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1722924"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1722924.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jow012" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2141473ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2141473" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1722924">jow012</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-30">04/30/24 15:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Personally, I believe this house got the hype because of how beautiful the bottles are. They MAKE you want to add it all to your collection. Are any of the scents from Parfums de Marley unique and niche enough for the price point? Honestly, I would say no. They are pretty mass appealing scents.<br />
<br />
But what they do very well is appeal to many people with effortless blends. I do have to admit that their scents are all still great and seem effortless. Almost none give me a headache which is so rare for me, and they actually last. Delina especially, I can't seem to think anyone would ever dislike it! Even if it's not unique - If everyone likes it, that still means it's a fantastic perfume. Having the most beautiful bottles is a plus. I wish that tassel was on the masculine line too.<br />
<br />
What I would say if you are thinking of getting this (since it is so expensive): what's most important is that you yourself love your perfume and you believe it reflects you. If you are willing to spend a lot on a high quality perfume, this is a delightful fruity rosy and feminine perfume that I can't see you regretting. It has a timeless quality to it. Id bet money that most people would continue to repurchase Delina specifically because it's so pleasant.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2141473"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2141473#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2140360" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Rhubarb as a note is always pungent and done wrong in my opinion, and it feels like litchi is the new hot note replacing cherry with how may perfumes have it- and again in all honesty- it smells sour in everything I’ve tried with it. The perfumers try to make it a new special never done before note and it really just isn’t that secret ingredient it used to be.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2072264">EauDeLa</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-23">04/23/24 09:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Roses with berries and cream on a bed of plastic babydoll skin (which they call "marshmallow"). This is the kind of fragrance that would have been found in a child's Christmas gift cosmetics set 30 years ago or in a glass strawberry bottle made by Avon. Perhaps its wild popularity is due to rampant nostalgia and the bleak times we find ourselves in. This is an uplifting, young, and fun scent that is best described as girly. It lacks sophistication and could easily be marketed as an Ariana Grande scent (which contain a lot of plastic doll/marshmallow). Packaging is certainly top notch, in line with its steep price. The darling pink bottle makes me happy just sitting there. Bottom line, though it is very nice, I do not think this one is worth the steep price tag. It isn't groundbreaking juice but lovely to own at a deep discount.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2133806"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2133806#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2127858" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2127858" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Baroqu3"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1265782"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1265782.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Baroqu3" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2127858ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2127858" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1265782">Baroqu3</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-17">04/17/24 17:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Delina! Delina! In my top 10 for life perfumes and I hope they don’t discontinue it.<br />
Delina was love at first sniff for and there’s no other rose perfume quite like this queen of roses!<br />
In the opening I get the litchi and rhubarb but it’s not sharp or tangy.<br />
It’s the most beautiful, light, dewy, pink and white rose mixture that is oh so feminine and modern. If you are scared of roses because you associate it with grandma or think it’s like rose water or tea rose then don’t worry because this is a pretty princess that is young, sweet, addictive and charming.<br />
The nutmeg and vanilla now joins the walls in the mid coupled with the litchi, bergamot and rhubarb. <br />
It is such a stunning delicious scent without being food like that lingers to the dry down as it gets more sweeter and it’s so smooth with nutmeg, peony and cashmere that it warm but not spicy.<br />
<br />
The vanilla is sweet and warm and oh so feminine, elegant yet alluring.<br />
This is easily 11/10 and i would recommend it as it’s perfect for leaving the most delicious scent trail and does it garner compliments.<br />
The great thing is that all the dupes are of the exclusive version and I can always tell the difference as delina original is very hard to dupe. None of the below mentioned perfumes smells like it, they are just rose perfumes. Delina is in a league of her own.<br />
I have only seen one dupe that managed to recreate this to a close 95% and it’s not listed below.<br />
If you have your pretty princess days get this!<br />
I’m almost out and will be unto bottle 2.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2127858"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2127858#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2126096" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2043694">Olenchyk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-05">04/05/24 05:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I love roses, but would have never thought of getting myself a rose perfume until I smelled, loved, and bought Fleur Musc by Narciso Rodriguez, which I repurchased several times (discontinued now). That one made me think I love rose perfumes, but I tried and completely disliked TF Rose Prick and Rose Magnetic by Essential Perfumes. In most other perfumes with rose notes in the mix, I can barely detect it. <br />
<br />
Delina is the first rose note comes very close to Fleur Musc for me, and is likeable for the same reasons. In fact, it's not just rose, it's the rose-peony-musc combo, in both. I sprayed both on different wrists and keep comparing a few hours on - both clean, pure, unsweetened rose-peony, very, very similar and I am really surprised noone has suggested this comparison before. But I still slightly prefer the Fleur Musc - it's ever so slightly purer and gentler. AND quite a bit less pricey (if you find it online in your country). <br />
<br />
To be sure, both are lovely scents for spring and summer, I always got compliments when I wore Fleur Musc in the office. Both have good projection, silage and longevity. In both perfumes, it's a photorealistic rose, making you feel like you're in an actual rose-peony garden, and not like you smeared some rose oil on top of your perfume.<br />
<br />
very nice just a notch of downgrade for the price tag</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2114973"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2114973#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2114184" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I wore this today and asked my mom what she thought. She got close to my wrist and wrinkled her nose. Apparently this smells like powdery old lady! Hahaha! The Delina die-hards would clutch their pearls right now! I asked her to smell it 2x more as it progressed and the 2nd time she smelled it, it apparently got better but she still decided on powdery old lady. I asked her to smell this because yesterday I wore Delina Exclusif for Easter and I wanted her to compare the 2. Well she complimented me the 1st time I ever wore DE but yesterday she said she couldn't smell me (but she can only smell really strong odors or faint ones really up close). So i sprayed Delina Ex on the card and let it dry and she said that it was less powdery and she liked it more than the other one (Delina). To me Delina has a nice juicy opening but the nutmeg is odd to me (I dont think I like it) especially since next I smell peony (a note that I dislike). The base to me is not super incensey (the Delina candle smells to me like a high quality fruity rose incense- just fantastic) but is more a soapy sweet vetiver. <br />
P.S. my mom is in her 50s and is not a perfumehead. She had never heard of Delina before i made her smell it and doesn't have social media to hear about it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2110596"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2110596#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2109980" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2108784" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Isabella Therese"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1337526"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1337526.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Isabella Therese" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Houbigant/Ambre-Rubis-97383.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.97383.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ambre Rubis"title="Ambre Rubis"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2108784ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2108784" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1337526">Isabella Therese</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-30">03/30/24 08:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Disclaimer: When I bought Delina, several years ago, I didn't know it was going to be so hyped. I don't have TikTok and at the time I had only heard one person on Youtube talk about it (and they just said it was a "pretty fragrance", that's it). I looked at the notes, found them to be interesting, bought a sample and liked it so much that I ended up buying a bottle. I didn't buy it just because someone hyped it up. Since a lot of people seem to think that people only like Delina because of the hype, I felt the need to clarify that it's not the case for me.<br />
So, here's my review:<br />
I don't know why this is always referred to as a rose scent, because it's a fruit explosion with a creamy base to my nose, and I also get way more peony than rose. Delina is tart, fruity and creamy. Without doubt a summer fragrance. To me one of the strongest notes here is elderflower, which is a little weird since it's not in there. I also get the litchi and the rhubarb, and on my skin it's not sour at all. Delina is a little floral too, but this is first and foremost a fruity fragrance. Much more complex that your usual fruity floral. It's a grown up version of a fruity summer fragrance. It smells elegant and expensive. Delina is very powerful, lasts for more than 12 hours on my skin and lasts forever on clothes (until you wash them). Strong projection too, a little goes a long way. It's expensive, but since you don't need to overspray you get a lot of bang for your buck. I only wear Delina in the summer (and maybe late spring), so I still have a lot of juice left in my 30 ml bottle. Wearing Delina always makes me happy. Quentin Bisch really is a great perfumer! 9.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2108784"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2108784#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2107958" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1975722">sweetlolly333</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-27">03/27/24 14:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Its meh for all the hype influencers are making it to be. It is neither groundbreaking nor is it "its own scent" something I had never smelt before. I can assure you if you'd been to the Middle East this is a very common scent of rose water and Oud. Scent- 10/10<br />
Longevity- 9/10<br />
Sillage- 5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="2102614"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=2102614#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2102552" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The fruit, nutmeg, and vanilla remind me of fruit crisp with vanilla ice cream. The nutmeg, vanilla, and cashmeran add a much-needed warmth. This scent is a great balance of powdery dewy florals, fresh juicy fruit, and that subtley spicy warm sweetness. If anyone’s worried about the incense, it’s suuuuuper subtle and I can only detect it because I know it’s there. I also sometimes get something that reminds me of wet cardboard. You see lychee being the 2nd-most voted note—"too fruity"; rhubarb being the 4th—"too much rhubarb"; rose being the primary note—"I dislike rose with a passion"!!<br />
I wish I can put emojis here because I was crying with laughter!<br />
<br />
This is probably the best fruity rose with sweet creamy background I've ever tried (and trust me, I've compared at least a dozen)—the rose itself smells pretty natural, and the tart freshness gives it a foresty feel akin to cassis (blackcurrant leaves). Also, if you don't sniff the fragrance within the first 2 minutes, maybe it won't "assault" you lol</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="1061484"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=1061484#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1030586" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1179166">LilyRose1</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-02-12">02/12/19 11:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was a blind buy. It could have been the most expensive mistake of my perfume life...<br />
<br />
I discovered this from the most lovely Demi Rawling and her channel on YouTube and honestly, after watching all of her videos where she has talked about this gem I was convinced - I would love this and went ahead and bought the full bottle from the only online shop where we can get PDM here in Sweden. Felt a little fun to take a risk like that. <br />
<br />
First - the bottle. It’s the most beautiful perfume bottle I’ve ever seen and the prettiest in all of my collection. The lid itself weighs more than a brick of gold. Feels expensive (as it is).<br />
<br />
When I first sniffed it I was so very intrigued. It had this fresh, feminine and crispy feel to it and I was seriously hesitant to spray this on my skin.<br />
<br />
On me this is a pretty flowery, fresh, litchi and rhubarb scent.  I don’t really detect any rose, maybe just a hint. It’s sweet but not at all like candylike gourmand scents. It leans more on the fresh/flowery side. I think it’s the rhubarb that makes this perfume so interesting. I’ve never smelled anything like it and it stands out in my collection.<br />
<br />
I’ve liked it from the start but once it hit my skin and really dried down I was sure - it’s a love for me. I feel so feminine, fresh and beautiful when I wear this and I imagine I could wear this one either in summer or winter. I actually can’t wait to try this beauty out in the summer. <br />
<br />
Longevity and silage is beast mode on me. And I’ve got like a trillion compliments when I’ve worn this the few days I’ve own it. It’s a perfect match for me and a very very successful blind buy. Stunning scent for sure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="1030586"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=1030586#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1028805" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; On the first impression, Delina did not impress me and honestly, I wasn't sure if I even liked it. <br />
I never smelled the rose everyone talked about(but my sister did) and I like rose scents, but I could clearly smell the litchi and the rhubarb. <br />
I decided I wanted to give it a fair shot, I wanted to try something new.<br />
<br />
Oh man, have I fallen head over heels with this fragrance and it gets more and more addictive to me every time I wear it.<br />
The litchi is sweet and mouthwatering, the rhubarb is sour and nostalgic, new and fresh flowers and the cosy muskiness is just stunning. It's so bright and crispy and a  beautiful spring/summer fragrance. It reminds me of Tahiti in the summer idk why.  Very feminine and elegant fragrance.<br />
Delina is a compliment getter and it seems to be a big crowd pleaser.<br />
<br />
I'm determined on buying a bottle one day.<br />
Now I'll just have to save up for a trip to Paris since shipping to my country will probably cost me in total 450-500 USD.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="1028805"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=1028805#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent898397" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I definitely approve of this!<br />

Sillage - arm and a half length for the first 2 hours, followed by an intoxicating scent trail. 10/10<br />
Versatility - Spring, Fall, cooler Summers and Warmer winters. I can see it being pulled off in the colder winters / heat of summer with controlled spray(s). 9/10<br />
Compliments - I want to lick my gf's neck. Ladies, if youre wearing Delina, I just might lick yours. 10/10<br />

My gf wants a full bottle. The rose/litchi/rhubarb was entirely too strong and nauseating. I tried to wear it 3x before I turned around and sold mine. Extremely sweet and tart- happy to get rid of it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="43871"comment_id="1201250"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Delina-43871.html?ccid=1201250#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1372736" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
